[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  AddressSanitizer detected a [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-byte write overflow of a stack buffer in [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`mg_json_get`. The overflow occurs at line [0m[1;36m186[0m[39m of `json.c`, where an index goes [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeyond the bounds of the local array `nesting`. The failure surfaces during a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing run under libFuzzer.[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Stack-buffer-overflow [0m[1;39m([0m[39mas classified by AddressSanitizer[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash stack shows the write out of bounds in `mg_json_get`, called via [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput` in `test/fuzz.c`.  [0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The local variable `nesting` in `mg_json_get` spans bytes [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m62[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The error [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicates an access at offset [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m, one byte past the buffer end.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The harness is invoking `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mfuzz[0m[39m` with `-[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m` on the single testcase, [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mloading no external seed corpus.  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Sanitizer shadow memory confirms the overflow is on the stack left redzone [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mregion around `nesting`.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A libFuzzer run against the `mongoose` codebase invoked [0m                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetermined by a macro [0m[1;39m([0m[39meither `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` or `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m        [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreappears at the identical location in `mg_json_get`. The overflow persists, [0m       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39marray.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Initial Issue[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer invokes `mg_json_get` via `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`, and [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAddressSanitizer aborts with:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ERROR: AddressSanitizer: stack-buffer-overflow on address [0m[33m...[0m[39m in mg_json_get [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/src/mongoose/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;92m186:28[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  WRITE of size [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m at [0m[33m...[0m[39m offset [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m in frame[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    #[0m[1;36m0[0m[39m [0m[33m...[0m[39m in mg_json_get [0m[35m/src/mongoose/src/[0m[95mjson.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m186[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[33m...[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  This frame has [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m [0m[1;35mobject[0m[1;39m([0m[39ms[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m62[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[32m'nesting'[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m131[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m <== Memory access at offset [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m overflows this [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvariable[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  ```[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The `nesting` array is allocated on the stack as `unsigned char [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`. The log indicates a write beyond its last valid byte.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No other red flags [0m[1;39m([0m[39mheap corruption, use-after-free[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m appear; the sole violation [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis the stack array overflow during JSON parsing.[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Patch Attempt[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe submitted patch makes three changes in `src/json.c` around line [0m[1;36m127[0m[39m:[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Array size adjustment**  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```diff[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - unsigned char nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   + unsigned char nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Object-opening depth check**  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```diff[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   + if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Array-opening depth check**  [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```diff[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   + if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mdepth >= MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m return MG_JSON_TOO_DEEP;[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   ```[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo other changes were made. The intention was to use a correctly named macro [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and to treat reaching the maximum allowed depth as an error[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrather than only exceeding it.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Post-Patch Fuzzer Log[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The fuzzer runs again with the same command-line parameters.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- AddressSanitizer still reports a stack-buffer-overflow in `mg_json_get` at the [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The stack frame inspection again shows `nesting` occupying `[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m32[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m62[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and a write [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat offset [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m, overflowing by one byte.[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The error trace and deduplication tokens are identical to the initial run.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Areas for Further Investigation[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mTo understand and address the root cause, the following parts of the codebase [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshould be examined:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Macro definitions**  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Compare `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` vs. `MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING` in the header files. Are[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthey defined differently or remain the same numeric value?[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Check if either macro reflects the intended maximum stack array length.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Depth-tracking logic in `mg_json_get`**  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Review every increment/decrement of the `depth` variable.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Ensure the guard against excessive depth is evaluated **before** any write to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth[0m[1;39m][0m[39m`.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Writes to the `nesting` array**  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Locate all assignments of the form `nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mdepth[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = [0m[33m...[0m[39m`. Confirm that they [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moccur only when `depth` is strictly less than the array’s length.[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Determine whether path parsing operations can skip the guard and still modify [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`nesting`.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Overall JSON path handling**  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Inspect how `ed`, `ci`, `ei`, and `pos` interact with `depth` to select when [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`nesting` entries are updated.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Look for indirect paths or loops that might push `depth` beyond the checked [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthreshold.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Test harness and fuzzer input patterns**  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - While the harness itself is not the root cause, analyze the kinds of JSON [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstrings the fuzzer generates to trigger this overflow. This may reveal corner cases[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the nesting logic.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA holistic view of these elements will clarify why the guard conditions are [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minsufficient and where the code must be tightened to prevent stack-buffer overflows[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `mg_json_get`.[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39marray `nesting` beyond its allocated size. A patch was attempted to replace the [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   →  [0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   `unsigned char nesting[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mMG_JSON_MAX_NESTING[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;`[0m                                    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial Issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fuzzer output shows a one-byte write beyond the end of the local array `nesting` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min `mg_json_get` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjson.[0m[1;92mc:186[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The crash stack trace:  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • `mg_json_get` writes past the buffer.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The buffer is allocated on the stack with size determined by [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH`.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • AddressSanitizer highlights a write at offset [0m[1;36m62[0m[39m into `nesting`, which only [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspans bytes [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m61[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mKey Observations  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The overflow is in the parsing loop of `mg_json_get`, which tracks nesting levels[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min a fixed-size array.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The error reproduces deterministically under libFuzzer, indicating malformed or [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdeeply nested JSON input triggers depth miscalculation.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The variable `nesting` is too small for certain inputs, and the depth guards [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`if[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mdepth > MAX[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m allow one iteration too many.  [0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch Attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The local array size was changed from `MG_JSON_MAX_DEPTH` to [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`MG_JSON_MAX_NESTING`.  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Depth checks were changed from `>` to `>=` to prevent incrementing beyond the [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmaximum allowed nesting.  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstack-buffer-overflow at the same code location [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjson.[0m[1;92mc:186[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfirming that array sizing or bounds checks remain incorrect.  [0m                   [2m                [0m
